</p><p>In February 2009, <a href="/wiki/Aymeric_Chauprade" title="Aymeric Chauprade">Aymeric Chauprade</a>, a professor of geopolitics at CID military college in Paris, was fired by French Defence Minister <a href="/wiki/Herv%C3%A9_Morin" title="Herv\xc3\xa9 Morin">Herv\xc3\xa9 Morin</a> for writing a book entitled <i>Chronicle of the Clash of Civilizations</i> that espoused 9/11 conspiracy theories.<sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261">&#91;260&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In September 2009, <a href="/wiki/Van_Jones" title="Van Jones">Van Jones</a>, an adviser to US President Barack Obama, resigned after his signature on a 2004 petition calling for an investigation into whether government officials deliberately allowed the 9/11 attacks to occur and other controversial statements came to light drawing criticism. Van Jones said he was a victim of a smear campaign, adding that he does not currently, nor ever has agreed with that theory.<sup id="cite_ref-ObamaDidNotOrderVanJonesResignation_262-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ObamaDidNotOrderVanJonesResignation-262">&#91;261&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The 9/11 truth movement became an issue in the 2010 Texas Gubernatorial Republican primary when candidate <a href="/wiki/Debra_Medina" class="mw-redirect" title="Debra Medina">Debra Medina</a> replied when asked by <a href="/wiki/Glenn_Beck" title="Glenn Beck">Glenn Beck</a> about US government involvement in the 9/11 attacks: "I think some very good questions have been raised in that regard, there are some very good arguments, and I think the American people have not seen all of the evidence there, so I have not taken a position on that." After being criticized for the remarks by opposing candidates, Medina said that she has never been a 9/11 truth movement member and believes the twin towers were attacked by Muslim terrorists.<sup id="cite_ref-263" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-263">&#91;262&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-264" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-264">&#91;263&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-left" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad_crop.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad_crop.jpg/180px-Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad_crop.jpg" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad_crop.jpg/270px-Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad_crop.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad_crop.jpg/360px-Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad_crop.jpg 2x" data-file-width="537" data-file-height="737" /></a><figcaption>Iranian president <a href="/wiki/Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad" title="Mahmoud Ahmadinejad">Mahmoud Ahmadinejad</a> made statements that were skeptical of al-Qaeda executing the 9/11 attacks.</figcaption></figure>
<p>On September 23, 2010, Iranian President <a href="/wiki/Mahmoud_Ahmadinejad" title="Mahmoud Ahmadinejad">Mahmoud Ahmadinejad</a> in a speech to the United Nations said that "[t]he majority of the American people, as well as other nations and politicians, believe [...] some segments within the U.S. government orchestrated the attack to reverse the declining American economy and its grips on the Middle East in order to save the <a href="/wiki/Zionist_entity" title="Zionist entity">Zionist regime</a>", and that "the majority of the American people as well most nations and politicians around the world agree with this view".<sup id="cite_ref-265" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-265">&#91;264&#93;</a></sup> The remarks prompted the United States delegation as well as others to walk out.<sup id="cite_ref-266" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-266">&#91;265&#93;</a></sup> U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> criticized Ahmadinejad\'s remarks before the United Nations General Assembly on the following day, saying that "[f]or him to make a statement like that was inexcusable" and called the remarks "offensive" and "hateful".<sup id="cite_ref-267" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-267">&#91;266&#93;</a></sup> Previously Ahmadinejad had described the 9/11 attacks as a "suspect event"<sup id="cite_ref-IranPresidentCastsDoubtOnSuspect911_268-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IranPresidentCastsDoubtOnSuspect911-268">&#91;267&#93;</a></sup> and suggested that the Bush Administration was involved in 9/11.<sup id="cite_ref-911MythsBusted_269-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-911MythsBusted-269">&#91;268&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AhmadinejadQuotes_270-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AhmadinejadQuotes-270">&#91;269&#93;</a></sup> The Iranian president repeated his claims in 2011 with another appearance at the UN and was thereafter criticized in an article appearing in al-Qaeda\'s magazine, <i><a href="/wiki/Inspire_(magazine)" title="Inspire (magazine)">Inspire</a></i>. The article claimed that Ahmadinejad was jealous of al-Qaeda because the stateless and under-fire Islamic terrorist organization did on 9/11 what Iran could not do.<sup id="cite_ref-271" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-271">&#91;270&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2012, Egyptian President <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Morsi" title="Mohamed Morsi">Mohamed Morsi</a> has called for a scientific conference to look into the events of 9/11 and speculated that the attacks were an inside job. According to an international poll that same year, huge majorities in Muslim countries prefer to believe baseless conspiracy theories rather than listen to the mainstream facts of what happened on September 11, 2001, in New York City and Washington. Although al-Qaeda occasionally brags about its "achievement," 75 percent of Egyptian citizens, for example, still deny that Arabs carried out the attacks, as a Pew study reported in July 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272">&#91;271&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Legal_cases">Legal cases</span></h2>
<p>Army specialist April Gallop filed suit claiming that Vice President <a href="/wiki/Dick_Cheney" title="Dick Cheney">Dick Cheney</a>, Secretary of Defense <a href="/wiki/Donald_Rumsfeld" title="Donald Rumsfeld">Donald Rumsfeld</a>, and other Bush administration officials orchestrated the 9/11 attacks and that the Pentagon was hit by an attack ordered by Cheney. The suit was dismissed in 2010 by Judge <a href="/wiki/Denny_Chin" title="Denny Chin">Denny Chin</a>, who said the claim was "the product of cynical delusion and fantasy". Her lawyers filed an appeal to the <a href="/wiki/U.S._Court_of_Appeals" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Court of Appeals">U.S. Court of Appeals</a> which in April 2010 issued a <a href="/wiki/Show_cause_order" class="mw-redirect" title="Show cause order">show cause order</a> why the lawyers and Gallop should not be sanctioned for filing a frivolous lawsuit. Her lawyers asked that the judges on the Court of Appeals recuse themselves because their emotions made them prejudge the case and abuse their power. On October 14, 2011, the judges sanctioned her lawyers $15,000 each for both the frivolous lawsuits and the accusations of prejudice. Gallop was not fined because of her unfamiliarity with the law.<sup id="cite_ref-273" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-273">&#91;272&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<li id="cite_note-147"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-147">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">A survey of the 1,700 victims whose religion was listed found approximately 10% were Jewish indicating around 270 in total. A survey based on the last names of victims found that around 400 (<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1154941027">.mw-parser-output .frac{white-space:nowrap}.mw-parser-output .frac .num,.mw-parser-output .frac .den{font-size:80%;line-height:0;vertical-align:super}.mw-parser-output .frac .den{vertical-align:sub}.mw-parser-output .sr-only{border:0;clip:rect(0,0,0,0);clip-path:polygon(0px 0px,0px 0px,0px 0px);height:1px;margin:-1px;overflow:hidden;padding:0;position:absolute;width:1px}</style><span class="frac" role="math">15<span class="sr-only">+</span><span class="num">1</span>&#8260;<span class="den">2</span></span>%) were possibly Jewish. A survey of 390 Cantor Fitzgerald employees who had public memorials (out of the 658 who died) found 49 were Jewish (<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1154941027"><span class="frac" role="math">12<span class="sr-only">+</span><span class="num">1</span>&#8260;<span class="den">2</span></span>%). According to the 2002 American Jewish Year Book, New York State\'s population was 9% Jewish. Sixty-four percent of the WTC victims lived in New York State.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. <li id="cite_note-FAZ_Videos-58"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-FAZ_Videos_58-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-FAZ_Videos_58-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1133582631"><cite class="citation news cs1"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.faz.net/artikel/C30721/terroranschlaege-neue-videos-vom-11-september-30306648.html">"Neue Videos vom 11. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">September 12,</span> 2010</span>. <q>Das private "International Center for 9/11 Studies" hatte erfolgreich auf Herausgabe der Videodokumente geklagt und sie nun auf seinem eigenen Kanal bei Youtube ver\xc3\xb6ffentlicht. [The private "International Center for 9/11 Studies" had successfully sued for release of the videos, and they have now published them on their own channel on Youtube.] Das "National Institute of Standards and Technology"&#160;... hatte die Videos&#160;... jahrelang nicht freigegeben. [The "National Institute of Standards and Technology"&#160;... had not released the videos for years.]&#160;... Die bislang unbekannten Videos sollen als weitere Beweise f\xc3\xbcr eine Verschw\xc3\xb6rung rund um den 11. September dienen. [The previously unknown videos are intended to serve as further evidence of a conspiracy surrounding September 11.]&#160;... [Many of the newly released videos show pictures of WTC7.]</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Frankfurter+Allgemeine+Zeitung&amp;rft.atitle=Neue+Videos+vom+11.+September+-New+videos+of+September+11&amp;rft.date=2010-09-10&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.faz.net%2Fartikel%2FC30721%2Fterroranschlaege-neue-videos-vom-11-september-30306648.html&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3A9%2F11+conspiracy+theories" class="Z3988"></span></span>
